focus_tree = {
	id = saudi_focus_tree
	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			add = 10
			tag = SAU
		}
	}

	default = no
	continuous_focus_position = { x = 0 y = 1000 }

	focus = {
		id = SAU_unif_gcc_council
		icon = gcc

		x = 53
		y = 0
		offset = {
			x = 0
			y = 5
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					tag = JOR
					tag = YEM
					tag = MOR
				}
			}
		}
		offset = {
			x = -38
			y = -2
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					tag = EGY
				}
			}
		}
		offset = {
			x = -18
			y = 2
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					tag = IRQ
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 5

		allow_branch = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = JOR
				original_tag = IRQ
				original_tag = YEM
				original_tag = MOR
				original_tag = EGY
				original_tag = SAU
				original_tag = QAT
				original_tag = UAE
				original_tag = BHR
				original_tag = KUW
				original_tag = OMA
			}
		}

		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		available = {
			has_idea = idea_gcc_member_state
			gcc_dominant_member = yes
			gcc_unity_greater_0 = yes
		}

		bypass = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = gcc_focus_completed_tt
				has_global_flag = SAU_unif_gcc_council_completed
			}
			has_idea = idea_gcc_member_state
		}

		completion_reward = {
			add_political_power = 75
			set_global_flag = SAU_unif_gcc_council_completed
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: focus SAU_unif_gcc_council executed"
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

	focus = {

						target = JOR

	focus = {
		id = SAU_FA_befriend_the_turks
		icon = align_to_turkey

		x = -1
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = SAU_FA_influence_muslim_europe

		cost = 4.3

		prerequisite = { focus = SAU_FA_influence_muslim_europe }
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = SAU_FA_contain_the_turks }

		available = {
			if = {

				no_jihadist_government = yes
			}
			country_exists = TUR
			NOT = { has_war_with = TUR }
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: focus SAU_FA_befriend_the_turks executed"
			news_event = { days = 45 id = gulf.14 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = support id = "TUR" value = 20 }
			add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = "TUR" value = 20 }
			TUR = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = diplomatic_support
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = strategic_reasons_support_tt
				add_ai_strategy = { type = support id = ROOT value = 20 }
				add_ai_strategy = { type = befriend id = ROOT value = 20 }
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1
				ROOT = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { influence_array^0 = TUR }
							check_variable = { influence_array_val^0 > 9.999 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { influence_array^1 = TUR }
							check_variable = { influence_array_val^1 > 9.999 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { influence_array^2 = TUR }
							check_variable = { influence_array_val^2 > 9.999 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { influence_array^3 = TUR }
							check_variable = { influence_array_val^3 > 9.999 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { influence_array^4 = TUR }
							check_variable = { influence_array_val^4 > 9.999 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { influence_array^5 = TUR }
							check_variable = { influence_array_val^5 > 9.999 }
						}
						AND = {
							check_variable = { influence_array^6 = TUR }
							check_variable = { influence_array_val^6 > 9.999 }
						}
					}
				}
